    not 1@ == 1

        0@ -= 1
        0085: 10@ = 0@ // (int)
        jump to @FUCKINGFUCK2

    end

    wait 2000
    
    for 0@ = 0 to 10@
    0AD3: v$LADDER_FILE2 = format "ld%d" 0@
    0AF2: 1@ = get_float_from_ini_file "data/ladders.ini" section v$LADDER_FILE2 key "UPX" 
    0AF2: 2@ = get_float_from_ini_file "data/ladders.ini" section v$LADDER_FILE2 key "UPY" 
    0AF2: 3@ = get_float_from_ini_file "data/ladders.ini" section v$LADDER_FILE2 key "UPZ"

    0AF2: 4@ = get_float_from_ini_file "data/ladders.ini" section v$LADDER_FILE2 key "DWX" 
    0AF2: 5@ = get_float_from_ini_file "data/ladders.ini" section v$LADDER_FILE2 key "DWY" 
    0AF2: 6@ = get_float_from_ini_file "data/ladders.ini" section v$LADDER_FILE2 key "DWZ"
    6@ += 0.5

    6@ > 900.0

    0AD9: write_formatted_text "18161, ladmarker, 1, %f, %f, %f, 0, 0, 0, 1, -1%c" in_file 28@ 1@ 2@ 3@ 0xA
    0AD9: write_formatted_text "18161, ladmarker, 1, %f, %f, %f, 0, 0, 0, 1, -1%c" in_file 28@ 4@ 5@ 6@ 0xA

    0AD9: write_formatted_text "18161, ladmarker, 0, %f, %f, %f, 0, 0, 0, 1, -1%c" in_file 28@ 4@ 5@ 6@ 0xA
    end     
    
    end

    0AD1: show_formatted_text_highpriority "ASS WRITED" time 1000
